***torpedo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a> (10801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">torpēdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a> fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">torpēdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">numbness, torpidity, electric <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>ray</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">torpeō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I am stiff, numb, torpid; I am astounded; I am inactive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-dō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noun suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see also Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">steorfan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στερεός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stereós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">solid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Lithuanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">tirpstu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become rigid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">трупети</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trupeti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:torpedo.html>torpedo</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">projectile adapted for underwater use</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A low-lying streamlined car.</li></ol>

***torsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a> (55751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pack, load</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare metathesized <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trossen.html>trossen</a></i>, meaning the same), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">torser</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pack, bind together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">trousser</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*torsare</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*torsus</i>, a variant form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tortus</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">torqueō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To carry or bear with difficulty.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>

***tosh.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a> (16453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From 19th-century British <a href = vnd.unilang:thieves.html>thieves</a>' cant, of uncertain origin. Sense of nonsense possibly influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tush</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nonsense! <a href = vnd.unilang:tsk.html>tsk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tsk.html>tsk</a>!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> attested from 15th century.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Copper; <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> made of copper
<ul><li><b>1851</b>, H. Mayhew, <i>London labour and the London poor</i>, II. 150/2
<dl><dd>The sewer-hunters <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> formerly, and indeed are still, called by the name of Toshers, the articles which they pick up in the course of their wanderings along shore being known among themselves by the general term ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>’, a word more particularly applied by them to anything made of copper.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Valuables retrieved from sewers and drains
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, J. <a href = vnd.unilang:aiken.html>Aiken</a>, <i>Midnight <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Place</i>, v. 164
<dl><dd>I am present engaged in fishing for <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> in the sewers of Blastburn.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Rubbish, trash, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> especially in the sense of nonsense, bosh, balderdash
<ul><li><b>1892 October 26</b>, <i>Oxford University Magazine</i>, 26/1
<dl><dd>To think what I've <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> through to hear that <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>! Frightful <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> it'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be, too.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1911</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._G._Wells" class="extiw" title="w:H. G. Wells">H. G. Wells</a>, <i>The New <a href = vnd.unilang:machiavelli.html>Machiavelli</a></i>, ch. 5,
<dl><dd>Perhaps it helped a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> into Parliament, Parliament still being a confused retrogressive corner in the world where lawyers and suchlike sheltered themselves from the onslaughts of common-sense behind a fog of Latin and Greek and twaddle and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1997</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J.K._Rowling" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J.K. Rowling">J.K. Rowling</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Harry Potter and the Philosopher | s Stone"><a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>Harry</a> Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, iv
<dl><dd>‘<a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>Took</a> yeh from the ruined house myself, on Dumbledore’s <a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>orders</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>Brought</a> yeh <a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> this lot...’</dd>
<dd>‘Load of old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>,’ <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Uncle Vernon.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic  school <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bath or foot pan
<ul><li><b>1881</b>, Leathes in C.E. Pascoe, <i>Everyday Life in our Public Schools</i>, ii. 20
<dl><dd>A ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>’ pan... <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also provided.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1905</b>, H. A. Vachell, <i>Hill</i>, i
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> call a tub a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Easy bowling
<ul><li><b>1898 June 25</b>, <i>Tit-Bits</i>, 252/3
<dl><dd>Among the recent neologisms of the cricket field <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>’, which means bowling of contemptible easiness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Used as a form of address</i>.
<ul><li><b>1954</b>, E. Hyams, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a> amp; Cream</i>, 175
<dl><dd>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>Ere</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>, you bin at <a href = vnd.unilang:cha.html>Cha</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a>?</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">toshy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">toshing</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To steal copper, particularly from ship hulls
<ul><li><b>1867</b>, W. H. Smyth, <i>Sailor's Word-book</i></li>
<li><i><b>Toshing</b></i>, a cant word for stealing copper sheathing from vessels' <a href = vnd.unilang:bottoms.html>bottoms</a>, or from dock-yard stores.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To search for valuables in sewers
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, J. <a href = vnd.unilang:aiken.html>Aiken</a>, <i>Midnight <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Place</i>, vi. 180
<dl><dd>You tend to the <b>toshing</b>, let Mester Hobday tend to the dealing.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic  school <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To use a tosh-pan, either to wash, to splash, or to "bath"
<ul><li><b>1883</b>, J.P. <a href = vnd.unilang:groves.html>Groves</a>, <i>From Cadet to <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a></i>, iii. 227
<dl><dd>‘<b>Toshing</b>’ <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the name given to a punishment inflicted by the cadets on any one of their number who made himself obnoxious. The victim, dressed in full <a href = vnd.unilang:uniform.html>uniform</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> forced to run the gauntlet of his brother cadets, who, as he passed, emptied the contents of their ‘tosh-cans’ (small baths holding about three <a href = vnd.unilang:gallons.html>gallons</a> of water) <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the wretched lad's head.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1903</b>, J. S. Farmer amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>., <i><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a></i>, VII. 171/1
<dl><dd>He <b>toshed</b> his house beak by mistake, and got three hundred.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tonce</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shorn, clipped</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tonsure</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">tosher</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">toshest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tight.
<ul><li><b>1776</b>, D. Herd, <i>Ancient amp; Modern Scottish <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a></i>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>Tosh</a></b></i>, tight, neat.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Neat, clean; tidy, trim.
<ul><li><b>1794</b>, J. Ritson, <i>Scottish <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a></i>, I. 99
<dl><dd>I <a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ay.html>ay</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fou.html>fou</a> clean and <a href = vnd.unilang:fou.html>fou</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b></dd>
<dd>As a' the neighbours can tell.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Comfortable, agreeable; friendly, intimate.
<ul><li><b>1821</b>, <i>Blackwood's Edinburgh Magazine</i>, 10 4
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> and agreeable company.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">toshy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">toshly</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Toshly: neatly, tidily
<ul><li><b>1808</b>, J. Mayne, <i>Siller Gun</i>, i. 20
<dl><dd>Shouther your arms!—O! <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> them <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> on, And not athraw!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshed</b>)
</p>

<ul><li><b>1826 November</b>, J. Wilson, <i>Noctes Ambrosianae</i>, xxix, in <i>Blackwood's Edinburgh Magazine</i>, 788
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo.html>Hoo</a> she wad try to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a> up</b>... her breest.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From 19th-century British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tosheroon</i>, from or alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tusheroon</i>, of uncertain derivation from British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">caroon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crown, a 5-shilling silver coin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mediterranean_Lingua_Franca" class="extiw" title="w:Mediterranean Lingua Franca">Sabir</a></span> and (originally) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">corona</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> either derived from or influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">madza caroon</i>, the British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> for the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mediterranean_Lingua_Franca" class="extiw" title="w:Mediterranean Lingua Franca">Sabir</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:mezzo.html>mezzo</a> corona</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">half-crown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly under influence from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="Etymology_1English"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">copper <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a>; valuables</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> above or from the half-crown's value of two <a href = vnd.unilang:shillings.html>shillings</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sixpence.html>sixpence</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A half-crown coin; its value
<ul><li><b>1933</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Orwell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George Orwell">George Orwell</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Down_and_Out_in_Paris_and_London" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Down and Out in Paris and London">Down and Out in Paris and London</a></i>, xxix
<dl><dd>‘’<a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>Ere</a> y’are, the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> rig-out you ever ’ad. A tosheroon [<a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a crown] for the coat, two ’ogs for the trousers, one and a <a href = vnd.unilang:tanner.html>tanner</a> for the boots, and a ’<a href = vnd.unilang:og.html>og</a> for the cap and scarf. That’s seven <a href = vnd.unilang:bob.html>bob</a>.’</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1961</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:eric.html>Eric</a> Partridge,  <cite>The Routledge Dictionary of Historical <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>tush</b> or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>. Money: <a href = vnd.unilang:cockney.html>Cockney</a>: late C.19–20. <a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>Ex</a>: <b>tusheroon</b>... But <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Camden_Hotten" class="extiw" title="w:John Camden Hotten">H.</a> errs, I believe: he should mean half-a-crown, for tusheroon and its C.20 variant tossaroon (2s. 6d.) are manifest corruptions of Lingua Franca MADZA CAROON.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1961</b>, J. Maclaren-Ross, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doomsday.html>Doomsday</a> Book</i>, i. v. 63
<dl><dd>Here's a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> to buy yourself some <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crown coin; its value
<ul><li><b>1859</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J.C._Hotten" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J.C. Hotten">J.C. Hotten</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Dictionary_of_Modern_Slang,_Cant,_and_Vulgar_Words" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Dictionary of Modern Slang, Cant, and Vulgar Words">A Dictionary of Modern <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a>, Cant, and Vulgar <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a></a></i>
<dl><dd><i>Half-a-crown</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known as an <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a></span>, <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a bull</span>, <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a <b>tusheroon</b></span>, and a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">madza caroon</span>; whilst a <i>crown</i> piece, or <i>five <a href = vnd.unilang:shillings.html>shillings</a></i>, may be called either a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">bull</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">caroon</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">cartwheel</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">coachwheel</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">thick-un</span>, or a <b><span style="font-variant:small-caps;">tusheroon</span></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1912</b>, J.W. Horsley, <i>I Remember</i>, xii. 253
<dl><dd>‘<b>Tush</b>’, for money, would be an abbreviation of ‘tusheroon’, which in old cant, and also in tinker dialect, signified a crown.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any money, particularly pre-decimalization British coinage</li></ol>
</body>

***tosti.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a> (32233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a></i>. First attested in the late 1950s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a>'s</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A toasted sandwich containing cheese, usually <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> and optionally other ingredients and condiments; a toastie.
<ul><li><b>1959</b> November 13, "Verwachtingsvolle <a href = vnd.unilang:harten.html>harten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sneller.html>sneller</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vamp.html>Vamp</a>;D in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Kalverstraat" (advertisement), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:parool.html>Parool</a></i>, page 24.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heerlijk.html>Heerlijk</a> b.v. <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a> (of <a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a>)</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Delicious for example for making <b>toasties</b> with <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> or cheese (or both)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***tot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> (117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tōte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tote</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">toti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">tōte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">zuo <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i>.
</p>

***totaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:totaal.html>totaal</a> (1394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">total</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tōtālis</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tōtus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all, whole, entire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin. Perhaps related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Oscan language">Oscan</a></span> <i class="Ital mention" lang="osc">𐌕𐌏𐌖𐌕𐌏</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="osc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">touto</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">community, city-state</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Umbrian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Umbrian language">Umbrian</a></span> <i class="Ital mention" lang="xum">𐌕𐌏𐌕𐌀𐌌</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xum-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">totam</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tribe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">acc.</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">þēod</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a nation, people, tribe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">thede</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Dutch</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:totdat.html>totdat</a> (966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> (98597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Emotionally moved (by), made to feel emotion (by).
<ul><li><b>1845</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benjamin_Disraeli" class="extiw" title="w:Benjamin Disraeli">Benjamin Disraeli</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Sybil/Book_4/Chapter_1" class="extiw" title="s:Sybil/Book 4/Chapter 1">Sybil</a></i>, Book 4, Chapter 1,
<dl><dd>"They say her Majesty <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> about these affairs of the Chartists than anything else," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a> Egerton.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1868</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louisa_May_Alcott" class="extiw" title="w:Louisa May Alcott">Louisa May Alcott</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Little_Women/Chapter_42" class="extiw" title="s:Little Women/Chapter 42">Little Women</a></i>, Part 2, Chapter 42: All Alone,
<dl><dd>“If there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> anything good or true in what I write, it isn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> mine. I owe it all to you and Mother and <a href = vnd.unilang:beth.html>Beth</a>,” <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jo.html>Jo</a>, more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> by her father’s <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> than by any amount of praise from the world.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1883</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jules_Verne" class="extiw" title="w:Jules Verne"><a href = vnd.unilang:jules.html>Jules</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verne.html>Verne</a></a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Hauteville (translator), <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Green_Ray/Chapter_XXI" class="extiw" title="s:The Green Ray/Chapter XXI">The Green <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a></a></i>, Chapter XXI: A Tempest in a Cavern,
<dl><dd>“And you <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to save <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a>,” answered Miss Campbell, more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> by the courage of the young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> than the dangers which could still happen.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Slightly mentally deficient; <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> in the head.
<ul><li><b>1913</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoevsky" class="extiw" title="w:Fyodor Dostoevsky">Fyodor Dostoevsky</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:eva.html>Eva</a> M. Martin (translator), <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Idiot/Part_III/Chapter_IV" class="extiw" title="s:The Idiot/Part III/Chapter IV">The Idiot</a></i>, Part III, Chapter IV,
<dl><dd>"Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you see he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a lunatic, prince?" whispered Evgenie Pavlovitch in his ear. "Someone <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> just now that he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a bit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> on the subject of lawyers, that he <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a mania for making <a href = vnd.unilang:speeches.html>speeches</a> and intends to pass the examinations. I am expecting a splendid burlesque now."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1922</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Joyce" class="extiw" title="w:James Joyce">James Joyce</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Ulysses_(novel)/Chapter_8" class="extiw" title="s:Ulysses (novel)/Chapter 8">Ulysses</a></i>, Episode 8: The Lestrygonians,
<dl><dd>All a bit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b>. Mad <a href = vnd.unilang:fanny.html>Fanny</a> and his other sister <a href = vnd.unilang:mrs.html>Mrs</a> Dickinson driving about with scarlet harness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***toujours.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a> (87225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">tousjours</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">toz jorz</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tuzjurz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without ceasing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all days</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tous</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">jours</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">altid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Replaced Old French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">sempres</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:semper.html>semper</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>always</li>
<li>still</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The "s" at the end of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a></i> will <b>not</b> trigger liaison. For example, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ici.html>ici</a></i> will be pronounced as <span class="IPA">[tu.ʒu.ʁ‿i.si]</span>.</li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">touwe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tou</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tawwą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:tau.html>Tau</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tou</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">tó</i> (Norwegian <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">to</i>).

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tôver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taubrą</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toveren.html>toveren</a> (9365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tôveren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōvaron</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taubrōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tover.html>tover</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toverij.html>toverij</a> (19521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toveren.html>toveren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to conjure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>sorcery</li></ol>

***tracer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a> (78883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">trace</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tracers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A compound, element, or isotope used to track the progress or history of a natural process.</li>
<li>A round of ammunition for a firearm that contains magnesium or another flammable substance arranged such that it will burn and produce a visible trail when fired in the dark.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a> ammunition</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a> bullet</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>The act or state of tracking or investigating something.
<ul><li><b>1964</b>, <i>Galaxy Magazine</i> (volume 23, issues 1-6, page 125)
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> have a five-man <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a></b> on him now. He's heading for a Vorster cell on Michigan Boulevard, and he's drunk as a lord. Should <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> intercept him?</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b>,  Joint Commission Resources,  <cite>Environment of Care <a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>Tracer</a> Workbook</cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 5:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A surveyor typically conducts a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a></b> on his or her own and <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> meets up with the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of the team to discuss findings.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  CardCaptorXP (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a>),  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://soundcloud.com/xp-muzik/from-the-sewers">From the Sewers</a>” | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://genius.com/Cardcaptorxp-from-the-sewers-lyrics">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Ain'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> never running but I'm a paper chasing<br />They gon catch up to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, they gon need a pacer<br />How they over-watching <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> without a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a></b></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A request to trace the movements of a person or an object, such as a shipment.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:claire.html>Claire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a>,  <cite>A Runway for a Dream</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The next morning when she awoke, she <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:darcy.html>Darcy</a> what <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> happened, and <a href = vnd.unilang:darcy.html>Darcy</a> agreed that she should go to the police and this time ask them if they could put a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tracer.html>tracer</a></b> on her incoming phone calls, just in case he called again.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A person who traces something.</li>
<li>A device or instrument used to assist in making tracings.</li></ol>

***trage.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trage.html>trage</a> (13701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*trāgi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trēgijaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum">trâge</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>slow, sluggish</li>
<li>slow, lazy</li>
<li>weak</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***tragedie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>tragedie</a> (4875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>tragedie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tragoedia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τραγῳδία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tragōidía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">epic play, tragedy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τράγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trágos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male goat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ᾠδή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ōidḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">song</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a reference to the goat-satyrs of the theatrical plays of the Dorians.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>tragedie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>tragediën</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>tragedies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>tragedietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">drama</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">tragedy</span>

***trainen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trainen.html>trainen</a> (2971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">train</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trainen.html>trainen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To train (teach, practice <a href = vnd.unilang:skills.html>skills</a>) an animal, especially for use at hunting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To train, <a href = vnd.unilang:coach.html>coach</a> a person or team, e.g. supervise exercices</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To train oneself (in ...)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be in training, (do) exercice(s)</li></ol>

<ul><li>(animals) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:africhten.html>africhten</a></span>, (falconry) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:treinen.html>treinen</a></span></li>
<li>(other people) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:coachen.html>coachen</a></span></li>
